## Top Concept: actual departure date (qualifier)
<a id='top-actual-departure-date-qualifier'></a>

### Concepts in this Section

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>actual departure date (qualifier)</span>
<a id='actual-departure-date-qualifier'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-12>
- **definition (@en):** qualifier indicating the date/time corresponds to the actual (realized) departure

## Top Concept: advice (documentary credit)
<a id='top-advice-documentary-credit'></a>

### Hierarchy
- <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[advice (documentary credit)](#advice-documentary-credit)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-296>)

### Concepts in this Section

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>advice (documentary credit)</span>
<a id='advice-documentary-credit'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-296>
- **definition (@en):** the authenticated communication of the terms and conditions of a documentary credit, or an amendment thereof, from the issuing bank to the beneficiary, usually transmitted via an advising bank
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[advising bank](#advising-bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-287>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[documentary credit](#documentary-credit)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-239>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[documentary credit beneficiary](#documentary-credit-beneficiary)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-86>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[issuing bank](#issuing-bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-286>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-advice-documentary-credit)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>customs office of guarantee</span>
<a id='customs-office-of-guarantee'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-55>
- **definition (@en):** customs office at which a guarantee used for customs transit is lodged and administered, including registration/management of the guarantee reference number (GRN) and reference amount
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[customs authority](#customs-authority)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-253>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[customs office](#customs-office)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-299>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[customs authority](#customs-authority)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-253>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[customs declaration](#customs-declaration)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-237>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[customs office of destination](#customs-office-of-destination)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-4>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[customs office of transit](#customs-office-of-transit)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-48>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[customs procedure](#customs-procedure)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-215>)

### Concepts in this Section

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>CITES appendix reference</span>
<a id='cites-appendix-reference'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-146>
- **definition (@en):** reference to the CITES listing category (Appendix I, II or III) under which a species is included; used to determine permitting and trade conditions
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[classification](#classification)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-306>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[annual quota](#annual-quota)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-116>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[CITES management authority](#cites-management-authority)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-372>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[CITES permit](#cites-permit)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-233>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[exported quantity](#exported-quantity)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-125>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[specimen country of origin](#specimen-country-of-origin)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-60>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[specimen country of re-export](#specimen-country-of-re-export)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-67>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>commodity classification</span>
<a id='commodity-classification'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-305>
- **definition (@en):** the systematic assignment of goods to a standardized classification scheme for the purposes of customs, trade statistics, transport, and regulatory compliance
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[classification](#classification)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-306>)
- **narrower:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[dangerous goods classification](#dangerous-goods-classification)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-307>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[HS code (commodity code)](#hs-code-commodity-code)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-188>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[customs declaration](#customs-declaration)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-237>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[description of goods](#description-of-goods)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-117>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[regulatory measure](#regulatory-measure)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-277>)

<a id='common-name'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-390>

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>dangerous goods classification</span>
<a id='dangerous-goods-classification'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-307>
- **definition (@en):** the assignment of substances, mixtures, or articles to standardized hazard classes, divisions, and ancillary attributes governing their safe transport, labeling, documentation, stowage, and handling
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[commodity classification](#commodity-classification)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-305>)

  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[tunnel restriction code](#tunnel-restriction-code)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-176>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Consignment](#consignment)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-193>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[flash point temperature](#flash-point-temperature)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-157>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[goods item](#goods-item)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-198>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[regulatory measure](#regulatory-measure)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-277>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>dangerous goods technical name</span>
<a id='dangerous-goods-technical-name'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-168>
- **definition (@en):** Proper shipping name, supplemented as necessary with the correct technical name, by which a dangerous substance or article may be correctly identified, or which is sufficiently informative to permit identification by reference to generally available literature

OR

A specific chemical/technical descriptor required to supplement the PSN for generic/N.O.S. entries; typically shown in parentheses after the PSN.

OR 

The additional chemical or biological name of a substance required in transport documentation and package markings when a proper shipping name is of the 'not otherwise specified' (n.o.s.) type. It identifies the constituent(s) that most contribute to the hazard.
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[dangerous goods information](#dangerous-goods-information)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-393>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[transport designation](#transport-designation)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-363>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Dangerous Goods](#dangerous-goods)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-217>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[N.O.S. entry](#n-o-s-entry)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-365>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[proper shipping name (PSN)](#proper-shipping-name-psn)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-364>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-classification)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>explosive compatibility group code</span>
<a id='explosive-compatibility-group-code'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-158>
- **definition (@en):** a one-letter code (A–S) that identifies the nature of explosives and prescribes which types may be safely stored and transported together, used in conjunction with hazard division numbers
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[code](#code)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-366>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[dangerous goods classification](#dangerous-goods-classification)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-307>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[dangerous goods declaration](#dangerous-goods-declaration)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-284>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>N.O.S. entry</span>
<a id='n-o-s-entry'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-365>
- **definition (@en):** a generic 'not otherwise specified' entry that may cover multiple substances/articles and typically requires a technical name to qualify the PSN

  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[transport designation](#transport-designation)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-363>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>tunnel restriction code</span>
<a id='tunnel-restriction-code'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-176>
- **definition (@en):** a code assigned under the ADR agreement that specifies restrictions on the passage of dangerous goods through tunnels, based on their risk of explosion, toxic release, or fire
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[code](#code)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-366>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[dangerous goods classification](#dangerous-goods-classification)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-307>)

  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[regulatory measure](#regulatory-measure)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-277>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[transport document](#transport-document)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-226>)

## Top Concept: code
<a id='top-code'></a>

### Hierarchy
- <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[code](#code)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-366>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[administrative reference code (ARC)](#administrative-reference-code-arc)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-259>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[currency code](#currency-code)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-261>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>special provision code</span>
<a id='special-provision-code'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-179>
- **definition (@en):** a code that identifies a special provision assigned in dangerous goods regulations to a specific UN number or class of substances, indicating exceptions, additional requirements, or conditions applicable to the transport of those goods

OR

a regime-specific reference (e.g., 274, 188, A123) to a dangerous goods special provision that further qualifies classification, naming, packaging, or marking requirements

## Top Concept: contract
<a id='top-contract'></a>

### Hierarchy
- <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[contract](#contract)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-303>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[contract term](#contract-term)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-360>)
    - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[payment term](#payment-term)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-148>)
      - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[payment due date](#payment-due-date)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-26>)
    - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[trade terms](#trade-terms)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-214>)
      - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[incoterm](#incoterm)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-213>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[transport contract](#transport-contract)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-302>)

### Concepts in this Section

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>contract</span>
<a id='contract'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-303>
- **definition (@en):** a legally enforceable agreement between two or more parties that creates mutual obligations, typically formed by offer, acceptance, and consideration, and containing terms that define rights, duties, and remedies
- **narrower:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[contract term](#contract-term)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-360>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[transport contract](#transport-contract)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-302>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[contract identifier](#contract-identifier)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-9>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[contractual conditions](#contractual-conditions)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-301>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Party](#party)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-196>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[service](#service)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-265>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-contract)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>contract term</span>
<a id='contract-term'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-360>
- **definition (@en):** a specific clause or agreed parameter in a contract, often standardized and codified for trade purposes
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[contract](#contract)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-303>)

[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>incoterm</span>
<a id='incoterm'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-213>
- **definition (@en):** a standard ICC-defined trade term allocating costs, risks, and responsibilities between seller and buyer
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[trade terms](#trade-terms)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-214>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-contract)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>payment due date</span>
<a id='payment-due-date'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-26>
- **definition (@en):** the calendar date by which a payment obligation must be settled under the agreed terms of a trade transaction
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[payment term](#payment-term)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-148>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-contract)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>payment term</span>
<a id='payment-term'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-148>
- **definition (@en):** identification of the terms of payment between the parties to a transaction (generic term)
or
the agreed conditions for the timing, method, and amount of payment for goods or services supplied.
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[contract term](#contract-term)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-360>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[trade terms](#trade-terms)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-214>)
- **narrower:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[payment due date](#payment-due-date)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-26>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[freight payer](#freight-payer)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-56>)

## Top Concept: DG aircraft limitation
<a id='top-dg-aircraft-limitation'></a>

### Hierarchy
- <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[DG aircraft limitation](#dg-aircraft-limitation)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-169>)

- **definition (@en):** dangerous goods permitted only on cargo aircraft
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[DG aircraft limitation](#dg-aircraft-limitation)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-169>)

[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>DG aircraft limitation</span>
<a id='dg-aircraft-limitation'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-169>
- **definition (@en):** a restriction indicating whether dangerous goods may be transported on both passenger and cargo aircraft, or only on cargo aircraft
- **narrower:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[cargo aircraft only](#cargo-aircraft-only)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-392>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[passenger and cargo aircraft](#passenger-and-cargo-aircraft)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-391>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-dg-aircraft-limitation)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>passenger and cargo aircraft</span>
<a id='passenger-and-cargo-aircraft'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-391>
- **definition (@en):** dangerous goods permitted on both passenger and cargo aircraft
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[DG aircraft limitation](#dg-aircraft-limitation)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-169>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-dg-aircraft-limitation)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>transport leg</span>
<a id='transport-leg'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-225>

<a id='top-financial-institution'></a>

### Hierarchy
- <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[financial institution](#financial-institution)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-246>)

### Concepts in this Section

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>advising bank</span>
<a id='advising-bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-287>
- **definition (@en):** a bank that advises the credit to the beneficiary, without obligation to honor it
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[bank role](#bank-role)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-285>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[advice (documentary credit)](#advice-documentary-credit)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-296>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[documentary credit](#documentary-credit)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-239>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[documentary credit beneficiary](#documentary-credit-beneficiary)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-86>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>available with (bank)</span>
<a id='available-with-bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-63>
- **definition (@en):** bank with which the documentary credit is stated to be available (issuing, confirming, or a nominated bank), as indicated in the credit
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[bank role](#bank-role)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-285>)
- **related:**

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>bank</span>
<a id='bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-245>
- **definition (@en):** a financial institution providing trade finance services such as letters of credit, collections, and guarantees
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[financial institution](#financial-institution)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-246>)

<a id='claiming-bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-295>

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>confirming bank</span>
<a id='confirming-bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-288>
- **definition (@en):** a bank that adds its confirmation (guarantee of payment) to the credit at the request of the issuing bank

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>negotiating bank</span>
<a id='negotiating-bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-294>
- **definition (@en):** a bank that examines and pays (or agrees to pay) against compliant documents under a credit, and seeks reimbursement from the issuing/confirming bank
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[bank role](#bank-role)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-285>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[available with (bank)](#available-with-bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-63>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[confirming bank](#confirming-bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-288>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[issuing bank](#issuing-bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-286>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[negotiation](#negotiation)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-334>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[seller's bank](#seller-s-bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-11>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-financial-institution)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>nominated bank</span>
<a id='nominated-bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-289>
- **definition (@en):** a bank authorized by the issuing bank in the credit to receive, examine, and/or pay against the beneficiary’s documents
- **broader:**

<a id='reimbursing-bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-290>

<a id='seller-s-bank'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-11>
- **definition (@en):** bank designated by the seller (beneficiary) to receive payment or to act in relation to the seller under the agreed payment method (e.g., open account, collections, or documentary credit)
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[bank role](#bank-role)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-285>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[bank](#bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-245>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[bank account](#bank-account)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-379>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[bank account identifier](#bank-account-identifier)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-54>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[buyer](#buyer)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-38>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[buyer's bank](#buyer-s-bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-91>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>dangerous goods technical name</span>
<a id='dangerous-goods-technical-name'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-168>
- **definition (@en):** Proper shipping name, supplemented as necessary with the correct technical name, by which a dangerous substance or article may be correctly identified, or which is sufficiently informative to permit identification by reference to generally available literature

OR

A specific chemical/technical descriptor required to supplement the PSN for generic/N.O.S. entries; typically shown in parentheses after the PSN.

OR 

The additional chemical or biological name of a substance required in transport documentation and package markings when a proper shipping name is of the 'not otherwise specified' (n.o.s.) type. It identifies the constituent(s) that most contribute to the hazard.
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[dangerous goods information](#dangerous-goods-information)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-393>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[transport designation](#transport-designation)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-363>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Dangerous Goods](#dangerous-goods)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-217>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[N.O.S. entry](#n-o-s-entry)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-365>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[proper shipping name (PSN)](#proper-shipping-name-psn)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-364>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>packing group</span>
<a id='packing-group'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-396>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-367>

<a id='proper-shipping-name-psn'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-364>
- **definition (@en):** the official name assigned to a dangerous goods entry for transport use
- **broader:**

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>Identifier</span>
<a id='identifier'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-221>
- **definition (@en):** a reference assigned to uniquely distinguish a document, consignment, shipment, or party
- **narrower:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[administrative reference code (ARC)](#administrative-reference-code-arc)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-259>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[bank account identifier](#bank-account-identifier)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-54>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[booking reference identifier](#booking-reference-identifier)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-2>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[contract identifier](#contract-identifier)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-9>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[conveyance reference number](#conveyance-reference-number)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-180>)

<a id='special-provision-code'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-179>

a regime-specific reference (e.g., 274, 188, A123) to a dangerous goods special provision that further qualifies classification, naming, packaging, or marking requirements

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>endorsement</span>
<a id='endorsement'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-332>
- **definition (@en):** the act of attesting to or transferring rights associated with a negotiable instrument or other document, typically by signature
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[documentary act](#documentary-act)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-331>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[negotiable transport document](#negotiable-transport-document)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-337>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[negotiation](#negotiation)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-334>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-legal-act)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>Legal act</span>
<a id='legal-act'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-330>
- **definition (@en):** an action with legal effect performed in the course of trade or transport (e.g., issuance, acceptance, endorsement
- **narrower:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[documentary act](#documentary-act)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-331>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[transfer of title](#transfer-of-title)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-335>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-legal-act)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>negotiation</span>
<a id='negotiation'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-334>
- **definition (@en):** the transfer of a negotiable instrument to another party, conferring rights to payment or to claim goods
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[documentary act](#documentary-act)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-331>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[endorsement](#endorsement)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-332>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[negotiable transport document](#negotiable-transport-document)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-337>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[negotiating bank](#negotiating-bank)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-294>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-legal-act)  
[⬆️ Back to Top](#index)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>transfer of title</span>
<a id='transfer-of-title'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-335>
- **definition (@en):** the legal transfer of ownership rights, often effected via endorsement of a negotiable document
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Legal act](#legal-act)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-330>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[negotiable transport document](#negotiable-transport-document)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-337>)

- **definition (@en):** Port, airport or other type of location at which a means of transport is scheduled to arrive or has arrived
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Location](#location)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-204>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>origin country</span>

- **definition (@en):** a location from or at which despatch is to take place; the facility or site where goods are handed over to the carrier for carriage
- **broader:**

### Hierarchy

  - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[package](#package)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-200>)
    - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[overpack](#overpack)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-319>)
    - <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>[shipping marks](#shipping-marks)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-139>)

### Concepts in this Section

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>logistics unit</span>
<a id='logistics-unit'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-201>
- **definition (@en):** a discrete, physically handled unit established for transport and/or storage, composed of one or more trade items or packages, intended to be moved, stored, or tracked as one
- **narrower:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[package](#package)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-200>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>overpack</span>
<a id='overpack'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-319>
- **definition (@en):** an enclosure used by a single consignor to contain one or more packages for ease of handling and stowage (e.g., shrink-wrapped pallet)

OR

an enclosure used to contain one or more packages to form a single handling unit
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[package](#package)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-200>)

### Concepts in this Section

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>cube volume</span>
<a id='cube-volume'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-134>
- **definition (@en):** a measurement normally arrived at by multiplying the maximum length, width and height of pieces or package or transport equipment
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[volume measure](#volume-measure)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-269>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>flash point temperature</span>
<a id='flash-point-temperature'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-157>
- **definition (@en):** lowest temperature at which a liquid emits sufficient vapour to ignite in air in the presence of an ignition source, determined under specified test conditions
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Measure](#measure)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-212>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>Q-value number</span>
<a id='q-value-number'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-162>
- **definition (@en):** a unique reference associated with a quantitative trade entitlement, such as a tariff quota allocation, used to identify the portion of goods eligible for preferential treatment or subject to quota limits in international trade transactions
OR
a calculated number used in dangerous goods regulations to determine whether different dangerous goods in limited quantities may be packed together in one outer package
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Quantity](#quantity)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-112>)
- **related:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[all packed in one information](#all-packed-in-one-information)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-167>)
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[Dangerous Goods](#dangerous-goods)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-217>)

[↩️ Back to Top Concept](#top-measure)

<a id='transport-means-gross-mass'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-281>
- **definition (@en):** the total mass of a transport means under defined conditions, typically including the mass of the vehicle or vessel, fuel, crew, passengers and load, unless otherwise specified

<a id='vessel-gross-tonnage-gt'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-282>
- **definition (@en):** the overall size of a vessel determined in accordance with the International Convention on Tonnage Measurement of Ships, 1969; a dimensionless index of internal volume

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>advance ruling</span>
<a id='advance-ruling'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-274>
- **definition (@en):** a binding decision issued by a customs authority or competent body, prior to importation or exportation, that provides certainty on the treatment of specific aspects of a trade transaction, such as tariff classification, origin determination, or customs valuation
- **broader:**

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>consignment summary description</span>
<a id='consignment-summary-description'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-119>
- **definition (@en):** a short textual description that summarizes the goods making up a consignment, intended to provide a clear and general characterization without item-level detail
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[description of goods](#description-of-goods)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-117>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>Consignment</span>
<a id='consignment'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-193>
- **definition (@en):** a batch of goods being transported under a single transport contract, identified for customs and commercial purposes
- **broader:**
  - <span style='font-size:1.1em;'>[trade transaction](#trade-transaction)</span> (<https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-194>)

#### <span style='font-size:1.3em;'>container utilization status</span>
<a id='container-utilization-status'></a>

- **IRI:** <https://iri.suomi.fi/terminology/a89c6af7a/concept-186>
- **definition (@en):** a trade and transport concept describing the degree to which a piece of transport equipment, such as a container or vehicle, is loaded with goods. Commonly expressed as “full,” “empty,” or “partly full,” this status is used in logistics, customs, and port operations to indicate handling, return, or cost conditions
